(§) ¥Í½¾Æ" ª?

asked the Minister of Foreign Affairs and Minister of Portsand Aviation:

(a) Will he admit that—

(i) malpractices do take place in the interviewsconducted for recruitments to the Sri LankaForeign Service; and

(ii) some of those who were recruited recently had beengiven incredible marks such as 150, 148 and 145at the interview?

(b) Will he take action to hold an inquiry into the aforesaidmatters?

(c) Will he state—

(i) the total approved cadre of the Sri Lanka ForeignService;

(ii) the seniority order updated as at January, 2006?

(iii) the number of vacancies existing at present in theForeign Service;

(iv) the number of officers recruited through the opencompetitive examinations held in 1994, 1995,1996, 1997, 1998, 1999, 2000, 2001, 2002, 2003and 2004; and

(v) Who they are?

(d) Will he present in this House in detail, the marksobtained by the aforesaid officers at the competitiveexamination and at the interview?

(e) If not, why?

asked the Minister of Healthcare and Nutrition :

(a) Will he inform this House —

(i) the number of part-time labourers who work in theSchool Dental Clinics in Sri Lanka; and

(ii) the names and addresses of them, separately?

(b) Will he take action to absorb these part time labourersinto the permanent service since they have alreadyworked for more than 190 days?

(c) If not, why?

asked the Minister of Railways and Transport and Ministerof Petroleum and Petroleum Resources Development :

(a) Is he aware that —

(i) Mr. N.C.S.P. Mendis who served as an ExecutiveOfficer, Grade IV in the Puttalam Depot of the SriLanka Transport Board has been transferred toAlawwa Depot situated around 100 kilometresaway from his home town following the 2004General Election;

(ii) salaries have not been paid to him from December2005 to March 2006;

(iii) a complaint had been made by Mr. Mendis toHuman Rights Commission in this regard?

(b) Will he state in this House —

(i) the reasons for subjecting him to this type ofinhuman treatment and illegal revenge who isacting as the Puttalam District Secretary and NorthWest Provincial Organizer of the Jathika SevakaSangamaya; and

(ii) whether steps will be taken to transfer Mr. Mendisback to the Puttalam Depot, reinstate him in thepreviously held position and pay due salaries witharrears?

(c) If not, why?

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)Mr. Speaker, the answer to the Question raised by theHon. Ranjith Aluvihare is as follows :

(a) (i) yes.

(ii) salary has been paid not taking into account nopay leave taken by Mr. Mendis. That excesspayment has been recovered during December2005 to March 2006.

(iii) Yes.

(b) (i) Does not arise.

(ii) If he will make an appeal it could be considered.

(c) Does not arise.

ªÇæ ÇâÔºà ¡õÍåïÚ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¼³Æ±È¶Æ £ßÄÇÍ¼)(The Hon. Ranjith Aluvihare)ªÇæ ¡æÄºøºëÄ¾ø, ÄÄ ¨åÇ¸Æ¨à ¼æ¾ª¾à¾ ¨æÄæºøÆú. ï ÄÍºàÄÆå Äå¾ÉÍú¨ ï¨åÌÄ´ ÈèÆå ºøïÂ¾Éå. ‘‘¦à¨ ÉæÇ¼úÆú’’ ¨øÆå ÀèÎèªºàïºåºà §ÂºëÄå§Íê´ ¾æÉº Û¨øÆåÉ ï¼¾Éå¼? Commission ¦¨´ ÈèÆå ºøïÂ¾Éå.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)¢ÈàÈéÄ¨à ¨Ç¾Éå ¾ ¦à ªæ¾ ÌÈ¨å ÂÈ¾Éå.

2006 §¨àïºåàÂÚ 0421552156

asked the Minister of Indigenous Medicine and DeputyMinister of Religious Affairs:

(a) Will he inform this House of —

(i) the sum of money which has been allocated by theMinistry of Religious Affairs for Muslim culturaland religious affairs in 2006;

(ii) the projects which are being implemented by theMinistry for developing Muslim cultural andreligious affairs;

(iii) the projects which are being contemplated as perthe above subject in due course; and

(iv) the sums of money which have already beenallocated and the sums which are intended forallocation, separately in respect of each project?

(b) Will he state —

(i) whether acts of fraud, corruption or irregularitieshave been reported in respect of the projects underimplementation at present; and

(ii) if so, what measures have been taken regardingthem?

(c) If not, why?

asked the Minister of Local Government and ProvincialCouncils:

(a) Will he state separately,—

(i) the Minsitries in the North Western ProvincialCouncil and Ministers in charge of theseMinistries;

ªÇæ Ç ¨Çæ¸å¾åÆ¨ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¼ ¯ÝµÇ·Ç»¯Æ¯)(The Hon. Ravi Karunanayake)This is accepted, but still the manner in which it was doneis not accepted. I will come to that, but now that you asked,there are eight or ten blocks that could be given for oilexploration. When you give one or two blocks for exploration,whethere it is to China, to America, to Cuba or North Korea,the valuation of the rest of the blocks falls to zero. That is theproblem. According to the maximum internationallypermissible and acceptable area of territorial waters of SriLanka, we can break it up to ten blocks. ªÇæ È¨àËàÄ¾à ¨øÖ¡æÈàÈ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¾¯Æº ¯È¼È©¾Æ¾)(The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella)ºÉÄ ¡Ìºñ ¨øÆ¾Éå. ¡Ìºñ ¨øÆÈå ¡Íê ïÉÈå, ¡Íê ïÉÈå ºÉºà ¡Ìºñ¨øÆ¾Éå. [Âå½å ¨×]

ªÇæ Ôº ïÍàÇºà ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¶ ÍÄ¼¶Æ)(The Hon. Vijitha Herath)ªÇæ ¾øïÆåà°ñ ¨»å¾åÆ¨ºëÄ¾ø, ¦ºëÄ¾àÈå ¡ºàÌ¾à ¨Î ªúÌêÄ´ ¡¾êÉ¼ºàº ï¼¾à¾ ÂæÍæ ¨øÉ´ ÀÌàïÌà, ¼ºàº ï¼¾à¾ ¾ ïÄ¾à¾ ïÄ ºæ¾´¦¾à¾ ¾çÆ ¨øÆå ºÄÆú ï¾åàÚÑÔÆå¾ê ¾ùºøÆ´ ¦¾à¾ ¨øï. ¦ºï¨å´¼ºàº ï¼¾à¾ ÂæÖ Æ´ ºÄÆú §ÂºëÄ¾àÈå ªúÌêÄ ¡ºàÌ¾à ¨Ç ºøÂêï¸à.¡¾à¾ ¦ºæ¾ ºÄÆú ï¾åàÚï´ Æ´ºà ïÉÈå ºøÂêï¸à. ¦à ï¾åàÚï ¾ùºøÆ´Æ´ºà É¾Éå ¾ ºÇÆú ¦à ¼ºàº ï¼¾àï¾à ¨øÆ¾ ºæ¾´ ¦¾à¾ Éêï¸à,§ÂºëÄ¾àÈå ¡ºàÌ¾à ¨ÇÀê ªúÌêï ºøÂê¸ê ÉæÛ¼à¼ ¾øÌÆú. ¦à ¾øÌå ºÄÆú ïÉª¾àºøÆ ¦¾àï¾à. ¡¾à¾ ¦à¨ ïºàÇæ ª¾à¾. ¦à¨Æú Äå ïÂåïÍåÄ ÀæÍæ¼úÈèÉÄºë ¨Ç¾àï¾à. ÌÃåÉ ï¾åÄ­ ÆæÑÄ¨à ¨Ìè ºæ¾¨ Ìè¼à½ ïÉÈå ¾æÍæ.ïÂåïÍåÄ ÀæÍæ¼úÈèÉ Äå ¦Æ ¾æÉº ¡É½åÇ¸Æ ¨Ç¾Éå. [Âå½å ¨ø×]

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)Hon. Deputy Speaker, I thank all the Members for theirvaluable contributions. It is the duty of His Excellency thePresident, the Government and the Opposition to use all theresources to exploit the possibility of extracting oil and gasas quickly as possible in order to build up the economy ofthis country. This is a national issue. I thank the formerPresident Chandrika Bandaranaike for initiating action inthis regard in the year 2001. During that period the thenChairman of the CPC, Mr. Anil Obeyesekere signed anagreement on 21st May, 2001 with TGS - NOPEC. Thereafter,Mr. Daham Wimalasena signed another non - exclusiveagreement on 13th February, 2002. The mandate of theagreement is to conduct seismic surveys to explore theprospects of petroleum resources in the territorial watersincluding the Exclusive Economic Zone of Sri Lanka.

[ªÇæ È¨àËàÄ¾à ¨øÖ¡æÈàÈ ÄÍºå]There are three objectives of the Agreement. They are asfollows :

1. To mandate TGS - NOPEC to conduct seismic surveyson behalf of the CPC to explore petroleum resourcesin the entire territorial waters.

2. To empower both parties to share the income earnedby selling seismic data.

3. To assign the right of selling non - exclusive seismicdata with TGS - NOPEC on behalf of the CPCcomplying with the phases of the Agreement.

After signing this Agreement, Petroleum Resources Act,No.266 of 2003 was passed in Parliament in order tostreamline the exploration of petroleum resources in SriLanka. Thereafter, activities in connection with theexploration of petroleum resources in Sri Lanka that werecarried out by the CPC have been assigned to PetroleumResources Development Committee and PetroleumResources Development Secretariat. Accordingly, these twoorganizations have been made responsible for theimplementation of the activities connected with prospectingfor oil and gas in offshore areas off the west coast ofSri Lanka.

Now, I have to work according to the Agreement that hasbeen signed. TGS - NOPEC has violated its conditions. Oneof the conditions they have violated is that they have notsupplied the data within the specific period. The second oneis not giving us our royalty. Therefore, we decided to cancelthe Agreement without destroying our image in theinternational community. You cannot simply cancelagreement the way somebody wants it to be done. Oilexploration is timely and it is very important to Sri Lanka foraccelerated economic growth. In South East Asia, othercountries are moving ahead of us discovering oil or gas. It isprobably the only way that we can move Sri Lanka forward.We have talked about oil exploration from the 1950s. Butnothing has happened yet. If we conduct explorations nowand discover oil, We may even be ahead of our neighbours.An agreement is a two - sided document and connot beviolated by one party. My Secretary and the Director - Generalwent to Perth to find a way to go forward with oil explorationbecause a court settlement or arbitration will take many years.Currently, Sri Lanka is paying US Dollars one billion for oilimports. It is very important that we search for oil and gasfields in the Sri Lankan offshore area. Any discovery willaccelerate the economic growth and the development of thecountry. This is why I am trying to expedite it.

TGS - NOPEC has invested US Dollars 5.5 million to getthe data. They, as an international company, have taken aconsiderable risk in spending this money to collect data.They expect an adequate return for their investment. Theirtarget is another US Dollars five million as return on theirinvestment. In addition, by cancelling the Agreement TGS -NOPEC will no longer have any exclusive rights to collect

22692270

2006 §¨àïºåàÂÚ 04

2D and 3D seismic data offshore Sri Lanka and they will losetheir chance to collect additional revenue further through2D and 3D seismic survey. Therefore, they will also lose therevenue expected by selling the data already collected untilthe year 2012. So, I simply cannot cancel the Agreement. Iwould like to ask the Hon. Vijitha Herath, now if we are goingto cancel the Agreement, do you suggest that no compensationshould be paid?

ªÇæ Ôº ïÍàÇºà ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¶ ÍÄ¼¶Æ)(The Hon. Vijitha Herath)

I think that we need not pay.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

Yes, I also can take up that position that we need not pay.But when we go to court and when the arbitration takes place,it will take more than 15years to finalize this. We will bepostponing this exploration for another 10 - 15 years.

ªÇæ Ôº ïÍàÇºà ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¶ ÍÄ¼¶Æ)(The Hon. Vijitha Herath)

Hon. Minister, they have already violated the Agreement.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

They have violated it, all right. We say that they are theonly people who have violated it. Just because they haveviolated it, can we cancel the agreement? What is theviolation? That is, not giving the data on time.

ªÇæ Ôº ïÍàÇºà ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¶ ÍÄ¼¶Æ)(The Hon. Vijitha Herath)

Yes.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

And not giving 5 per cent to us. These are two matters.

ªÇæ Ôº ïÍàÇºà ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¶ ÍÄ¼¶Æ)(The Hon. Vijitha Herath)

They have not paid the first instalment.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

But, does that warrant the cancellation of the Agreement?That is the first issue. All right. Secondly, what happens? Wecancel the Agreement, will we get the data? They will notgive the data. They will say, “Go to hell. You give us money.

Otherwise, we will not give the data.” Then, we have to go tocourt. This is why I sent my Director - General and the Secretaryto negotiate with them. The only area they have alreadysurveyed is the Mannar Basin including the Cauvery Basinand we wanted to tell them, “You better go ahead with that.We will do the balance.”

ªÇæ È¨àËàÄ¾à ¨øÖ¡æÈàÈ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¾¯Æº ¯È¼È©¾Æ¾)(The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella)That settlement is good.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

Yes. It is a very good settlement that I proposed. Up to nowwe have not spent a cent even.Without spending a cent wewanted this TGS - NOPEC to go ahead. So, I submitted aCabinet paper expecting the Cabinet to give me the blessings.But, unfortunately, due to various parties interfering in this,they got the Cabinet not to agree to it. So, it was decided thatwe give a block to India and a block to China on nomination.Not only on nominations, but we are also getting a signaturebonus of US Dollars 10 million each and also US Dollars 100million as a deposit. Government to government you cansell this. According to the law also you need not call fortenders.We can even call for applications. But that is not thesolution. What we were trying to do was to build up oureconomy. We thought that this was the best and the quickestway that we could do it. Otherwise, you have to sell the data.Then, you have to go for the 3D survey. Then, you have to gofor bidding. All these things will take time. I had prepared aschedule by which by now I would have called for tenders.

ªÇæ È¨àËàÄ¾à ¨øÖ¡æÈàÈ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¾¯Æº ¯È¼È©¾Æ¾)(The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella)We went through your settlement in the COPE. Thatsettlement is very good.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

Yes. But, Unfortunately I was told to cancel the Agreement.So, to cancel the Agreement, we appointed the CANC andgot legal opinion also. They have now decided to cancel theAgreement on the condition that we pay US Dollars 10.5million. Out of the US Dollars 10.5million, US Dollars 2million that they have already collected by sale of the datawill be deducted. Then, we have to pay US Dollars 8.5 million.So, that is the recommendation that is going before theCabinet this evening and I hope that will be gone throughbecause His Excellency the President himself said, “You haveto pay compensation.” We connot simply say, “Go, fly a kite”.I mean, a lot of money has been spent and just because theyhave violated some conditions, you cannot tell them that weare not going to pay. Then they will also say, “Okay, we are

22712272

ÀåÚÈèï¾àºëÉ

not going to give you the data.” So, where do we stand?Without the data can we proceed? Can we sell the data withouthaving it with us? So, this is the situation that we have tothink about. Just because of these disputes we are having weshould not oppose TGS - NOPEC like that. We must also bepractical in these matters.

We do not have professionals in the PRDS. Already I haveprepared the papers and we are creating 20 positions in thisfields including lawyers, economists, geologists andgeophysicists. This cadre has been approved but, the salarieset cetera have not been approved yet. So, once that is approveswe will appoint these officers.

It is not an easy task. Oil exploration needs massiveinvestment. To do the 3D seismic survey, having taken itover from TGS - NOPEC, we will have to find money. Even tofind US Dollars 10 million is not an easy task. That is thecompensation that we are going to pay. But, the view of mostpeople is, “You cancel it. Do not pay anything” Some peoplesay, “You cancel it. Pay US Dollars 10 million.” So, I ambetween the devil and the deep blue sea. But, we must bepractical in these matters.

Not only the money but also we do not have the technology.We can simply cancel it but then we will be blamedinternationally. Nobody will come to invest in this country.No one will accept Sri Lanka as a genuine country to comeand invest.

ªÇæ È¨àËàÄ¾à ¨øÖ¡æÈàÈ ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¾¯Æº ¯È¼È©¾Æ¾)(The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella)

They will think that this is not a trustworthy country.

ªÇæ ¦à. ¦. ¦. ÏÉêÌè ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ª° ©±Æ° ©ºÆ° Ì¹¿ÃÈ)(The Hon. A. H. M. Fowzie)

Yes, they will think that this is not a trustworthy country.So, we have to be very careful. We cannot do this just becausesome people want this to be cancelled.

The Cabinet paper that I submitted will be taken up today.The following recommendations are there in that.

The first one is, to pay US Dollars 8.5 million to TGS -NOPEC in addition to the US Dollars 2 million earned byselling Mannar Basin seismic data to acquire by PRDC, allthe Mannar Basin seismic data held by that company, and tocancel all agreements signed by TGS - NOPEC with theCeylon Petroleum Corporation.

ªÇæ Ä¾àºòéºëÄå, ¡¼ ¨æ¾ ¦¨´ ¢¼úÖÀºà ¨Ç¾ Äïªà ïÆåà°¾åÉ ï¨Æú.§¨àï¨åÄ ÈèÆ¾ 10.5¨à É¾à¼ú ïªÉå ÌÀìÚ¸ ¼ºàº - data - ¡À ÈÂåª¾à¾´Æú. ¼æ¾´ ¨ë¸Èå ïÌåÆå ïª¾ ºøïÂ¾ ÈèÆ¾ 2 ¡¶ê ¨Ç ÈèÆ¾8.5¨à ïªÉ¾à¾´Æ ¨øÆåÆú.

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available forRs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to theSUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 32, Transworks House,Lotus Road, Colombo 1. The fee should reach him on or bvefore November 30 each year.Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.
